–ö–∞–∫ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å –∏ –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å OAuth-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ Replit

–ù–∏–∂–µ ‚Äî –æ—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π, –ø–æ—à–∞–≥–æ–≤—ã–π –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–æ–∫. –û–Ω –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –¥–ª—è –ª—é–±–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ OAuth (Google, GitHub, –Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å, –í–ö –∏ —Ç.–¥.). –í–∞—à–∞ –∫–∞—Ä—Ç–∏–Ω–∫–∞ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ (–∏–ª–∏ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏), –∫—É–¥–∞ –≤—ã –≤–Ω–æ—Å–∏—Ç–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ, –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞. –í Replit —ç—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –∫–∞–∫ —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã (env) –∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ.

1) –û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ –∏ –∑–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É–π—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ

–ü–µ—Ä–µ–π–¥–∏—Ç–µ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å–∞ –∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ ¬´OAuth App¬ª/¬´Credentials¬ª:

Google: Google Cloud Console ‚Üí Credentials ‚Üí OAuth client ID

GitHub: Settings ‚Üí Developer settings ‚Üí OAuth Apps

–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å: OAuth.yandex.ru ‚Üí –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ

–í–ö–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–µ: dev.vk.com ‚Üí –ú–æ–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è ‚Üí Standalone/Website App

–ü—Ä–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–∏ —É–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—é—Ç—Å—è:

Redirect URI (Callback URL) ‚Äî –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å, –Ω–∞ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä –≤–µ—Ä–Ω—ë—Ç –∫–æ–¥ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏.

–í Replit Redirect URI –≤—ã–≥–ª—è–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–∞–∫

–ï—Å–ª–∏ —É –≤–∞—Å Express/Flask –Ω–∞ Replit:

https://<–∏–º—è-—Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞>.<–≤–∞—à-–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback


(–∏–ª–∏ –ª—é–±–æ–π –≤–∞—à –ø—É—Ç—å, –≥–ª–∞–≤–Ω–æ–µ ‚Äî —Å–æ–ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Å —Ä–æ—É—Ç–æ–º –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ)

–í–∞–∂–Ω–æ: URI –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—Ç—å –≤–ø–ª–æ—Ç—å –¥–æ —Å–∏–º–≤–æ–ª–∞ —Å —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞.

2) –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è

–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –≤—ã –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ:

Client ID (–ò–î –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞)

Client Secret (–°–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞)

Authorization URL (URL-–∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏)

Token URL (URL-–∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–∞)

Scope (–û–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è/–†–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è) ‚Äî —Å–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –ø—Ä–∞–≤ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–æ–≤.

–≠—Ç–∏ –ø–æ–ª—è –≤—ã –∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç–µ –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ (–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ–º —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω—à–æ—Ç–µ) –∏/–∏–ª–∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç–µ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ.

–¢–∏–ø–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è URL (–¥–ª—è —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫–∏)
–ü—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä	Authorization URL	Token URL	–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä scope
Google	https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/v2/auth	https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token	openid email profile
GitHub	https://github.com/login/oauth/authorize	https://github.com/login/oauth/access_token	read:user user:email
–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å	https://oauth.yandex.ru/authorize	https://oauth.yandex.ru/token	login:email login:info
–í–ö	https://oauth.vk.com/authorize	https://oauth.vk.com/access_token	email –∏ –Ω—É–∂–Ω—ã–µ scope
3) –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ Client ID/Secret –≤ Replit –∫–∞–∫ —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã

–í Replit ‚Üí Secrets:

OAUTH_CLIENT_ID = –≤–∞—à Client ID

OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET = –≤–∞—à Client Secret

–ø—Ä–∏ –∂–µ–ª–∞–Ω–∏–∏: OAUTH_AUTH_URL, OAUTH_TOKEN_URL, OAUTH_SCOPE, OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI

–ù–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –∫–æ–º–º–∏—Ç—å—Ç–µ —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã –≤ —Ä–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–π ‚Äî –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ Secrets.

4) –ù–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ –∫–æ–¥ –≤ Replit
–í–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç A. Node.js (Express, –±–µ–∑ –≤–Ω–µ—à–Ω–∏—Ö –±–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫ ‚Äî –º–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä)
// index.js
const express = require("express");
const fetch = require("node-fetch"); // ^3
const qs = require("querystring");

const app = express();

const CLIENT_ID = process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_ID;
const CLIENT_SECRET = process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET;
const AUTH_URL = process.env.OAUTH_AUTH_URL;      // –Ω–∞–ø—Ä. Google/GitHub/–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å
const TOKEN_URL = process.env.OAUTH_TOKEN_URL;    // –Ω–∞–ø—Ä. Google/GitHub/–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å
const REDIRECT_URI = process.env.OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI || "https://<–∏–º—è-—Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback";
const SCOPE = process.env.OAUTH_SCOPE || "openid email profile";

app.get("/", (req, res) => {
  res.send(`<a href="/auth">–í–æ–π—Ç–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ OAuth</a>`);
});

app.get("/auth", (req, res) => {
  const params = new URLSearchParams({
    response_type: "code",
    client_id: CLIENT_ID,
    redirect_uri: REDIRECT_URI,
    scope: SCOPE,
    // state –ø–æ-—Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–µ–º—É –Ω–∞–¥–æ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è—Ç—å
  });
  res.redirect(`${AUTH_URL}?${params.toString()}`);
});

app.get("/auth/callback", async (req, res) => {
  const { code } = req.query;
  if (!code) return res.status(400).send("–ù–µ—Ç –∫–æ–¥–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏");

  // –û–±–º–µ–Ω –∫–æ–¥–∞ –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω
  const body = {
    grant_type: "authorization_code",
    code,
    redirect_uri: REDIRECT_URI,
    client_id: CLIENT_ID,
    client_secret: CLIENT_SECRET, // –¥–ª—è GitHub –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∏ –≤ —Ç–µ–ª–µ, –∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Basic
  };

  const resp = await fetch(TOKEN_URL, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded", "Accept": "application/json" },
    body: qs.stringify(body),
  });

  const token = await resp.json();
  // token.access_token, token.id_token (—É OpenID), token.refresh_token –∏ —Ç.–ø.
  res.send(`<pre>${JSON.stringify(token, null, 2)}</pre>`);
});

app.listen(3000, () => console.log("http://localhost:3000"));

  }

–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ—â–µ ‚Äî –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ passport (passport-google-oauth20, passport-github2), –Ω–æ –≤—ã—à–µ ‚Äî –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–∞—è ¬´—É—á–µ–±–Ω–∞—è¬ª —Å—Ö–µ–º–∞.

–í–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç B. Python (Flask + authlib)
# main.py
from flask import Flask, redirect, request, url_for
from authlib.integrations.flask_client import OAuth
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = os.environ.get("FLASK_SECRET_KEY", "change-me")

oauth = OAuth(app)
oauth.register(
    name="provider",
    client_id=os.environ["OAUTH_CLIENT_ID"],
    client_secret=os.environ["OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET"],
    access_token_url=os.environ["OAUTH_TOKEN_URL"],
    authorize_url=os.environ["OAUTH_AUTH_URL"],
    client_kwargs={"scope": os.environ.get("OAUTH_SCOPE", "openid email profile")}
)

@app.route("/")
def index():
    return '<a href="/login">–í–æ–π—Ç–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ OAuth</a>'

@app.route("/login")
def login():
    redirect_uri = os.environ.get("OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI", "https://<–∏–º—è-—Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback")
    return oauth.provider.authorize_redirect(redirect_uri)

@app.route("/auth/callback")
def auth_callback():
    token = oauth.provider.authorize_access_token()
    return f"<pre>{token}</pre>"

app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=3000)


poetry/requirements: Flask, Authlib

5) –ß—Ç–æ –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å –≤ ¬´–ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥ –æ–±–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–æ–≤¬ª

–í –≤–∞—à–µ–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–µ –¥–≤–∞ –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç–∞:

–ü–æ —É–º–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω–∏—é (–∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å POST) ‚Äî –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—á–∞ client_id/client_secret –≤ —Ç–µ–ª–µ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∞ (application/x-www-form-urlencoded). –ü–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤—É (Google, –Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å).

–ó–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–∫ –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–æ–π –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ ‚Äî Authorization: Basic base64(client_id:client_secret). –¢–æ–∂–µ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ (GitHub –ø—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç –æ–±–∞ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–∞). –ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω-—ç–Ω–¥–ø–æ–∏–Ω—Ç –≤ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç Basic ‚Äî –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞–π—Ç–µ —ç—Ç–æ—Ç —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º.

6) –ß–∞—Å—Ç—ã–µ –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏

–ù–µ—Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ Redirect URI ‚Äî 90% –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ –ø—É—Ç—å –∏ —Å—Ö–µ–º—É https.

–ù–µ–æ–ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π/–Ω–µ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π OAuth-–∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç (Google) ‚Äî –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ Publishing Status –∏ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—ã—Ö –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π.

Scopes –Ω–µ —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—é—Ç ‚Äî –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ —Ä–æ–≤–Ω–æ —Ç–µ, —á—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω—ã –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–æ–º.

–°–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ ‚Äî —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –≤ Replit Secrets, –∞ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ —á–∏—Ç–∞–π—Ç–µ process.env/os.environ.

7) –ö–∞–∫ ¬´–≤–∑—è—Ç—å —ç—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ Replit¬ª

–ò—Ö –Ω–µ–ª—å–∑—è ¬´–≤–∑—è—Ç—å –∏–∑ Replit¬ª ‚Äî –≤—ã –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç–µ –∏—Ö –æ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ (—à–∞–≥ 2), –∑–∞—Ç–µ–º:

–≤–Ω–æ—Å–∏—Ç–µ –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ (–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ–º —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω—à–æ—Ç–µ),

–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç–µ Client ID/Secret –≤ Replit ‚Üí Secrets,

–ø—Ä–æ–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç–µ AUTH_URL, TOKEN_URL, SCOPE, REDIRECT_URI –≤ Secrets –∏–ª–∏ .env.

–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–¥ –≤ Replit –Ω–∞—á–Ω—ë—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—Ç—å –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π OAuth-—Ñ–ª–æ—É.

–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Å–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç–µ, –∫–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å (Google/GitHub/–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å/–í–ö –∏ —Ç.–¥.), –¥–∞–º –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤—ã–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è URL, –º–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π scope –∏ —Ç–æ—á–Ω—ã–π Redirect URI —Å –≤–∞—à–∏–º –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω–æ–º Replit.

–í—ã —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∏:
—è –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–∞—à–µ–ª . –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ –ø–æ —à–∞–≥–æ–≤–æ –æ–±—å—è—Å–Ω–∏
ChatGPT —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª:
–î—É–º–∞–ª –Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç—è–∂–µ–Ω–∏–∏ 19s

–ù–∏–∂–µ ‚Äî –ø–æ—à–∞–≥–æ–≤–∞—è, –æ—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏—è: –∫–∞–∫ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å OAuth-–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏ –ø–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å –∏—Ö –≤ Replit. –°–∫—Ä–∏–Ω –≤—ã—à–µ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ —Ç–æ –æ–∫–Ω–æ: —Ç–∞–º —Ä–µ—Ñ–µ—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∞. –í–∞–º –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å OAuth-–ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ (Google/GitHub/–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å/–í–ö –∏ —Ç.–ø.), –≤–∑—è—Ç—å –æ—Ç—Ç—É–¥–∞ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏ –≤–Ω–µ—Å—Ç–∏ –∏—Ö –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç –Ω–∞ Replit.

1. –û–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞

–ö–æ–≥–æ –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –¥–ª—è –≤—Ö–æ–¥–∞: Google, GitHub, –Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å, –í–ö–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–µ –∏ —Ç.–¥. –û—Ç –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å–∞ –≤—ã –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ:

Client ID (–ò–î –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞)

Client Secret (–°–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞)

Authorization URL (URL –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏)

Token URL (URL —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–∞)

Scope (–û–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è/—Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è)

2. –£–∑–Ω–∞–π—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à –≤–Ω–µ—à–Ω–∏–π URL –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞ (–¥–ª—è Redirect URI)

–í Replit –æ—Ç–∫—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ –Ω—É–∂–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–ø–ª ‚Üí Run ‚Üí —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∞ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∞ Open in new tab.
–°–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä—É–π—Ç–µ –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å –≤–∏–¥–∞:

https://<slug-–ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞>.<–≤–∞—à-–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co


–ï—Å–ª–∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç–µ Deployments ‚Äî –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –ø–æ–¥–¥–æ–º–µ–Ω *.replit.app. –û–±–∞ –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç–∞ –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω—ã.
Redirect URI —Ä–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É–µ–º:

https://<slug>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback


–≠—Ç–æ—Ç –ø—É—Ç—å /auth/callback –≤—ã —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑—É–µ—Ç–µ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ. –ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –≤ —Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—Ç—å —Å —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ —É–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç–µ —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞.

3. –ó–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É–π—Ç–µ OAuth-–ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞
3.1. Google

–ó–∞–π–¥–∏—Ç–µ –≤ Google Cloud Console ‚Üí APIs & Services ‚Üí Credentials.

–°–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–π—Ç–µ OAuth consent screen (—Ç–∏–ø External), –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—ã—Ö –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π (–ø–æ–∫–∞ —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–≤–∏–∫).

Create Credentials ‚Üí OAuth client ID ‚Üí —Ç–∏–ø ¬´Web application¬ª.

–í —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ Authorized redirect URIs –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à:

https://<slug>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback


–°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç–µ –∏ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ Client ID –∏ Client Secret.

URL‚Äô—ã –∏ —Å–∫–æ—É–ø—ã Google:

TOKEN_URL: https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token
SCOPE:     openid email profile

Authorization callback URL:

https://<slug>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback

3.3. –Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å

https://oauth.yandex.ru ‚Üí –ú–æ–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è ‚Üí –ó–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ.

–¢–∏–ø ¬´–í–µ–±-—Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å—ã¬ª.

Callback URL:

https://<slug>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback

URL‚Äô—ã –∏ —Å–∫–æ—É–ø—ã –Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å:

3.4. –í–ö–æ–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Ç–µ

https://dev.vk.com ‚Üí –ú–æ–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è ‚Üí –°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å (—Ç–∏–ø Website).

–ë–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–π –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω: –≤–∞—à –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω Replit (–±–µ–∑ –ø—É—Ç–∏).

Redirect URI:

https://<slug>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback

URL‚Äô—ã –∏ —Å–∫–æ—É–ø—ã –í–ö:

4. –ó–∞–Ω–µ—Å–∏—Ç–µ —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã –≤ Replit (–æ—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ)

–í–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–∏ –≤–∞—à–µ–≥–æ —Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞:

–õ–µ–≤–∞—è –ø–∞–Ω–µ–ª—å ‚Üí Secrets (Environment variables) (–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∫–∞ –∑–∞–º–∫–∞).

–î–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ (–∏–º–µ–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Ç–∞–∫–∏–º–∏):

OAUTH_CLIENT_ID = (Client ID)

OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET = (Client Secret)

OAUTH_AUTH_URL = (Authorization URL)

OAUTH_TOKEN_URL = (Token URL)

OAUTH_SCOPE = (–Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä —Å–∫–æ—É–ø–æ–≤, —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –ø—Ä–æ–±–µ–ª)

OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI = https://<slug>.<–Ω–∏–∫>.repl.co/auth/callback

–°–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –∫–æ–º–º–∏—Ç–∏–º –≤ –∫–æ–¥. –¢–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Secrets.

5. –ü–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç–µ –∫–æ–¥ (–º–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –∏ –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–æ)
–í–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç A: Node.js (Express)

–ü–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –ø—É—Ç—å –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–µ:
/index.js (–≤ –∫–æ—Ä–Ω–µ —Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞)
/package.json (–≤ –∫–æ—Ä–Ω–µ —Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞)

/index.js:

const express = require("express");
const fetch = require("node-fetch");
const qs = require("querystring");

const app = express();

const CLIENT_ID = process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_ID;
const CLIENT_SECRET = process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET;
const AUTH_URL = process.env.OAUTH_AUTH_URL;
const TOKEN_URL = process.env.OAUTH_TOKEN_URL;
const REDIRECT_URI = process.env.OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI;
const SCOPE = process.env.OAUTH_SCOPE || "openid email profile";

app.get("/", (req, res) => {
  res.send('<a href="/auth">–í–æ–π—Ç–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ OAuth</a>');
});

app.get("/auth", (req, res) => {
  const params = new URLSearchParams({
    response_type: "code",
    client_id: CLIENT_ID,
    redirect_uri: REDIRECT_URI,
    scope: SCOPE,
    // –†–ï–ö–û–ú–ï–ù–î–£–ï–¢–°–Ø: –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å state –∏ —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ –≤ —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–∏
  });
  res.redirect(`${AUTH_URL}?${params.toString()}`);
});

app.get("/auth/callback", async (req, res) => {
  const { code } = req.query;
  if (!code) return res.status(400).send("–ù–µ—Ç –∫–æ–¥–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏");

  const body = {
    grant_type: "authorization_code",
    code,
    redirect_uri: REDIRECT_URI,
    client_id: CLIENT_ID,
    client_secret: CLIENT_SECRET,
  };

  const resp = await fetch(TOKEN_URL, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
      "Accept": "application/json"
    },
    body: qs.stringify(body),
  });

  const token = await resp.json();
  res.send(`<pre>${JSON.stringify(token, null, 2)}</pre>`);
});

app.listen(3000, () => console.log("Server on http://localhost:3000"));

    "node-fetch": "^3.3.2",
    "querystring": "^0.2.1"
  }
}

–í–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç B: Python (Flask + Authlib)

–ü–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –ø—É—Ç—å –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–µ:
/main.py (–≤ –∫–æ—Ä–Ω–µ —Ä–µ–ø–ª–∞)

from flask import Flask
from authlib.integrations.flask_client import OAuth
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = os.environ.get("FLASK_SECRET_KEY", "change-me")

oauth = OAuth(app)
oauth.register(
    name="provider",
    client_id=os.environ["OAUTH_CLIENT_ID"],
    client_secret=os.environ["OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET"],
    access_token_url=os.environ["OAUTH_TOKEN_URL"],
    authorize_url=os.environ["OAUTH_AUTH_URL"],
    client_kwargs={"scope": os.environ.get("OAUTH_SCOPE", "openid email profile")},
)

@app.route("/")
def index():
    return '<a href="/login">–í–æ–π—Ç–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ OAuth</a>'

@app.route("/login")
def login():
    redirect_uri = os.environ["OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI"]
    return oauth.provider.authorize_redirect(redirect_uri)

@app.route("/auth/callback")
def callback():
    token = oauth.provider.authorize_access_token()
    return f"<pre>{token}</pre>"

app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=3000)


–ó–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏: Flask, Authlib (–¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –≤ requirements.txt).

6. –ß—Ç–æ –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å –≤ ¬´–ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥ –æ–±–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–æ–≤¬ª

–í –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞/–±–∏–±–ª–∏–æ—Ç–µ–∫–∏:

–ü–æ —É–º–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω–∏—é (POST) ‚Äî client_id/client_secret –≤ —Ç–µ–ª–µ x-www-form-urlencoded. –ü–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç Google/–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å.

Basic Auth –∑–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–∫ ‚Äî Authorization: Basic base64(client_id:client_secret). –ß–∞—Å—Ç–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è GitHub. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –≤ –¥–æ–∫–∞—Ö –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω Basic ‚Äî –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞–π—Ç–µ –µ–≥–æ.

7. –ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞

–ó–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç –≤ Replit (Run).

–û—Ç–∫—Ä–æ–π—Ç–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—É / ‚Üí –Ω–∞–∂–º–∏—Ç–µ ¬´–í–æ–π—Ç–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ OAuth¬ª.

–ü—Ä–æ–π–¥–∏—Ç–µ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞.

–ï—Å–ª–∏ –≤—Å—ë –≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ, –Ω–∞ /auth/callback —É–≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç–µ JSON —Å access_token (–∏, –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ, id_token, refresh_token).

8. –¢–∏–ø–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ –æ—à–∏–±–∫–∏ –∏ –∏—Ö –æ—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è

–ù–µ—Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞–µ—Ç Redirect URI ‚Üí –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å—Ç–µ –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω/–ø—É—Ç—å/https.

Google: –Ω–µ –æ–ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–æ–≤–∞–Ω —ç–∫—Ä–∞–Ω —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–∏—è ‚Üí –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ —Ç–µ—Å—Ç–æ–≤—ã—Ö –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π –∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–π–¥–∏—Ç–µ –ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é.

–ù–µ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω—ã–µ scopes ‚Üí –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–π—Ç–µ —Ä–æ–≤–Ω–æ –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞–µ–º—ã–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–æ–º.

–°–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ ‚Üí –ø–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–µ—Å–∏—Ç–µ –≤ Secrets.

–†–∞–∑–Ω—ã–µ –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω—ã (Run vs Deploy) ‚Üí –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –æ–±–∞ Redirect URI —É –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞.

9. –ß—Ç–æ –∑–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—Ç—å –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–µ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ–º —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω–µ (¬´–ê—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è¬ª)

–ò–î –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ ‚Äî –∏–∑ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ (Client ID).

–°–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ ‚Äî –∏–∑ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ (Client Secret).

URL-–∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ ‚Äî —Å–º. —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã –≤—ã—à–µ (AUTH_URL).

URL-–∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–∞ ‚Äî —Å–º. —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã –≤—ã—à–µ (TOKEN_URL).

–û–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è ‚Äî —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ–º—ã–µ —Å–∫–æ—É–ø—ã (–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä: openid email profile).

–ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥ –æ–±–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–æ–≤ ‚Äî –ø–æ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ (–æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ POST).

–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Å–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç–µ, –∫–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ –≤—ã–±–∏—Ä–∞–µ—Ç–µ (Google/GitHub/–Ø–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å/–í–ö), —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É –¥–∞–º –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤—ã–π –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–π –¥–ª—è –∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è (Redirect URI –ø–æ–¥ –≤–∞—à –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω Replit, —Å–∫–æ—É–ø—ã, –∏ —Ç–æ—á–Ω—É—é –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏—é –ø–æ –ø—É–Ω–∫—Ç–∞–º –º–µ–Ω—é —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞).

import express, { type Request, Response, NextFunction } from "express";
import { registerRoutes } from "./routes";
import { setupVite, serveStatic, log } from "./vite";

const app = express();
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: false }));

app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  const path = req.path;
  let capturedJsonResponse: Record<string, any> | undefined = undefined;

  const originalResJson = res.json;
  res.json = function (bodyJson, ...args) {
    capturedJsonResponse = bodyJson;
    return originalResJson.apply(res, [bodyJson, ...args]);
  };

  res.on("finish", () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    if (path.startsWith("/api")) {
      let logLine = ${req.method} ${path} ${res.statusCode} in ${duration}ms;
      if (capturedJsonResponse) {
        logLine +=  :: ${JSON.stringify(capturedJsonResponse)};
      }

      if (logLine.length > 80) {
        logLine = logLine.slice(0, 79) + "‚Ä¶";
      }

      log(logLine);
    }
  });

  next();
});

(async () => {
  const server = await registerRoutes(app);

  app.use((err: any, _req: Request, res: Response, _next: NextFunction) => {
    const status = err.status || err.statusCode || 500;
    const message = err.message || "Internal Server Error";

    res.status(status).json({ message });
    throw err;
  });

  // importantly only setup vite in development and after
  // setting up all the other routes so the catch-all route
  // doesn't interfere with the other routes
  if (app.get("env") === "development") {
    await setupVite(app, server);
  } else {
    serveStatic(app);
  }

  // ALWAYS serve the app on the port specified in the environment variable PORT
  // Other ports are firewalled. Default to 5000 if not specified.
  // this serves both the API and the client.
  // It is the only port that is not firewalled.
  const port = parseInt(process.env.PORT || '5000', 10);
  server.listen({
    port,
    host: process.env.HOST || "0.0.0.0",
  }, () => {
    log(serving on port ${port});
  });
})();

–û—Ç–∫—Ä–æ–π —Ñ–∞–π–ª server/routes.ts.

–°–∫–∞–∂–∏ ¬´–æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–ª¬ª, –∏ –¥–∞–º —Ç–æ—á–Ω—ã–π –±–ª–æ–∫ –∫–æ–¥–∞ –¥–ª—è –≤—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∫–∏ (–¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–º –¥–≤–∞ –º–∞—Ä—à—Ä—É—Ç–∞: /auth/github –∏ /auth/callback, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—Ç —Ç–≤–æ–∏ OAUTH_* —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç—ã).

import type { Express } from "express";
import { createServer, type Server } from "http";
import multer from "multer";
import path from "path";
import { storage } from "./storage";
import { setupAuth, isAuthenticated } from "./replitAuth";
import { insertPostSchema, insertDocumentSchema, insertAdSchema, insertBidSchema, insertSectionSchema, insertSubsectionSchema, insertNotificationSchema } from "@shared/schema";
import { cacheMiddleware, invalidateCache } from "./middleware/cache";
import { apiLimiter, createLimiter, authLimiter } from "./middleware/rateLimiter";
import { setupModerationRoutes } from "./routes/moderation";
import express from "express";

// Admin middleware
const requireAdmin = async (req: any, res: any, next: any) => {
  try {
    if (!req.user?.claims?.sub) {
      return res.status(401).json({ message: "Unauthorized" });
    }
    
    const user = await storage.getUser(req.user.claims.sub);
    if (!user || user.role !== 'admin') {
      return res.status(403).json({ message: "Admin access required" });
    }
    
    req.adminUser = user;
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Admin middleware error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ message: "Authentication error" });
  }
};

// Configure multer for file uploads
const uploadStorage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: (req, file, cb) => {
    cb(null, 'uploads/');
  },
  filename: (req, file, cb) => {
    const uniqueSuffix = Date.now() + '-' + Math.round(Math.random() * 1E9);
    cb(null, file.fieldname + '-' + uniqueSuffix + path.extname(file.originalname));
  }
});

const upload = multer({ 
  storage: uploadStorage,
  limits: {
    fileSize: 10 * 1024 * 1024, // 10MB limit
  },
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = /jpeg|jpg|png|gif|pdf|doc|docx|xls|xlsx|ppt|pptx|mp4|avi|mov|wmv|mp3|wav/;
    const extname = allowedTypes.test(path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase());
    const mimetype = allowedTypes.test(file.mimetype);
    
    if (mimetype && extname) {
      return cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(new Error('File type not allowed'));
    }
  }
});

export async function registerRoutes(app: Express): Promise<Server> {
  // –°—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è —Ä–∞–∑–¥–∞—á–∞ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–≤—ã—Ö —Ñ–∞–π–ª–æ–≤
  app.use('/games', express.static('games', {
    maxAge: '1d', // –ö—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ 1 –¥–µ–Ω—å
    etag: true,
    lastModified: true
  }));

  // Auth middleware
  await setupAuth(app);

  // –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º rate limiting –∫–æ –≤—Å–µ–º API —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∞–º
  app.use('/api', apiLimiter);
  app.use('/api/auth', authLimiter);

  // Auth routes
  app.get('/api/auth/user', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const user = await storage.getUser(userId);
      res.json(user);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching user:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch user" });
    }
  });

  // Sections routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/sections', cacheMiddleware(300), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const sections = await storage.getSections();
      res.json(sections);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching sections:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch sections" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/sections/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const section = await storage.getSection(req.params.slug);
      if (!section) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Section not found" });
      }
      res.json(section);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching section:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch section" });
    }
  });

  // Subsections routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/subsections', cacheMiddleware(300), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const sectionId = req.query.sectionId as string;
      const subsections = await storage.getSubsections(sectionId);
      res.json(subsections);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching subsections:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch subsections" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/subsections/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsection = await storage.getSubsection(req.params.slug);
      if (!subsection) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Subsection not found" });
      }
      res.json(subsection);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching subsection:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch subsection" });
    }
  });

  // Posts routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/posts', cacheMiddleware(180), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const offset = parseInt(req.query.offset as string) || 0;
      const posts = await storage.getPosts(subsectionId, limit, offset);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch posts" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/posts/featured', cacheMiddleware(600), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 5;
      const posts = await storage.getFeaturedPosts(limit);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching featured posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch featured posts" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/posts/popular', cacheMiddleware(300), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 5;
      const posts = await storage.getPopularPosts(limit);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching popular posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch popular posts" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/posts/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const post = await storage.getPost(req.params.slug);
      if (!post) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Post not found" });
      }
      
      // Increment views
      await storage.incrementPostViews(post.id);
      
      res.json(post);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching post:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch post" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/posts', isAuthenticated, createLimiter, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const postData = insertPostSchema.parse({ ...req.body, authorId: userId });
      const post = await storage.createPost(postData);
      
      // –ò–Ω–≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∫—ç—à –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ–≤
      invalidateCache('/api/posts');
      
      res.status(201).json(post);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error creating post:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to create post" });
    }
  });

  // Search routes
  app.get('/api/search', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const query = req.query.q as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      
      if (!query) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Search query is required" });
      }
      
      const posts = await storage.searchPosts(query, limit);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error searching posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to search posts" });
    }
  });

  // Documents routes
  app.get('/api/documents', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const documents = await storage.getDocuments(subsectionId, limit);
      res.json(documents);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching documents:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch documents" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/documents/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const document = await storage.getDocument(req.params.slug);
      if (!document) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Document not found" });
      }
      res.json(document);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching document:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch document" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/documents/:id/download', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      await storage.incrementDocumentDownloads(req.params.id);
      res.json({ message: "Download count incremented" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error incrementing download count:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to increment download count" });
    }
  });

  // Photo albums routes
  app.get('/api/photo-albums', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const albums = await storage.getPhotoAlbums(subsectionId, limit);
      res.json(albums);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching photo albums:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch photo albums" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/photo-albums/:slug', async (req, res) => {

  // Marketplace routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)

  app.get('/api/marketplace/ads', cacheMiddleware(120), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const categoryId = req.query.categoryId as string;

      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;

  app.get('/api/marketplace/ads/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {

      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }
      
      // Increment views
      await storage.incrementAdViews(ad.id);
      
      // Get bids for this ad
      const bids = await storage.getBids(ad.id);
      
      res.json({ ...ad, bids });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch ad" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/marketplace/ads', isAuthenticated, createLimiter, async (req: any, res) => {

      invalidateCache('/api/marketplace/ads');

  // Bid routes
  app.post('/api/marketplace/ads/:adId/bids', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const adId = req.params.adId;
      const bidData = insertBidSchema.parse({ ...req.body, adId, supplierId: userId });
      const bid = await storage.createBid(bidData);
      
      // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —É–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(adId);
      if (ad) {
        await storage.createNotification({
          userId: ad.userId,
          title: '–ù–æ–≤–∞—è –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ',
          message: –ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ "${ad.title}",
          type: 'info',
          linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
          adId: adId,
          bidId: bid.id
        });
      }
      
      res.status(201).json(bid);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error creating bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to create bid" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/marketplace/ads/:adId/bids', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const bids = await storage.getBids(req.params.adId);
      res.json(bids);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching bids:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch bids" });
    }
  });

  // Accept/Reject bid routes
  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:bidId/accept', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const bidId = req.params.bidId;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad || ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized" });
      }
      
      // –ü—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ–º –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É –∏ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      await storage.acceptBid(bidId, ad.id);
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: '–í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–æ!',
        message: –í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–æ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–æ,
        type: 'success',
        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
        adId: ad.id,
        bidId: bidId
      });
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤
      const allBids = await storage.getBids(ad.id);
      for (const otherBid of allBids) {
        if (otherBid.id !== bidId) {
          await storage.createNotification({
            userId: otherBid.supplierId,
            title: '–í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞–Ω–æ',
            message: –ü–æ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é "${ad.title}" –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞–Ω–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ,
            type: 'info',
            linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
            adId: ad.id,
            bidId: otherBid.id
          });
        }
      }
      
      res.json({ message: "Bid accepted successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error accepting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to accept bid" });
    }
  });

  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:bidId/reject', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const bidId = req.params.bidId;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad || ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized" });
      }
      
      // –û—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω—è–µ–º –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É
      await storage.rejectBid(bidId);
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—â–∏–∫–∞
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: '–í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–æ',
        message: –í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–æ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–æ,
        type: 'warning',
        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
        adId: ad.id,
        bidId: bidId
      });
      
      res.json({ message: "Bid rejected successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error rejecting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to reject bid" });
    }
  });

  // Close ad without selecting winner
  app.put('/api/marketplace/ads/:adId/close', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const adId = req.params.adId;
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(adId);
      if (!ad || ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized" });
      }
      
      // –ó–∞–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      await storage.closeAd(adId);
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Å–µ—Ö —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤
      const bids = await storage.getBids(adId);
      for (const bid of bids) {
        await storage.createNotification({
          userId: bid.supplierId,
          title: '–û–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ',
          message: –û–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–æ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ –±–µ–∑ –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è,
          type: 'info',
          linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
          adId: adId,
          bidId: bid.id
        });
      }
      
      res.json({ message: "Ad closed successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error closing ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to close ad" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/admin/media/upload', isAuthenticated, requireAdmin, upload.array('files', 10), async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const files = req.files as Express.Multer.File[];
      const uploadedFiles = [];
      
      for (const file of files) {
        const mediaData = {
          fileName: file.originalname,
          fileUrl: /uploads/${file.filename},
          fileSize: file.size,
          fileType: file.mimetype,
          uploadedBy: req.adminUser.id
        };
        const media = await storage.createMedia(mediaData);
        uploadedFiles.push(media);
      }
      
      res.status(201).json(uploadedFiles);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error uploading files:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to upload files" });
    }
  });

  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:id/accept', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const bidId = req.params.id;
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }

      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }

      if (ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized to manage this ad" });
      }

      await storage.acceptBid(bidId);
      
      // Create notification for accepted supplier
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: "–í–∞—à–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–∞!",
        message: –í–∞—à–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º.,

        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug}
      });

      res.json({ message: "Bid accepted successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error accepting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to accept bid" });
    }
  });

    try {
      const bidId = req.params.id;
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }

      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);

        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });

        title: "–ó–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–∞",
        message: –í–∞—à–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–∞ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º.,

      });

      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to reject bid" });
    }

  app.put('/api/marketplace/ads/:id/close', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const adId = req.params.id;
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(adId);
      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }

      if (ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized to manage this ad" });
      }

      await storage.closeAd(adId);
      
      // Create notifications for all bidders
      const bids = await storage.getBidsForAd(adId);
      for (const bid of bids) {
        if (bid.status === 'pending') {
          await storage.createNotification({
            userId: bid.supplierId,
            title: "–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç",
            message: –ó–∞–∫–∞–∑ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º –±–µ–∑ –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è.,
            type: "info",
            linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug}
          });
        }
      }

      res.json({ message: "Ad closed successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error closing ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to close ad" });
    }
  });



  app.post('/api/notifications', isAuthenticated, requireAdmin, async (req: any, res) => {

    }

    try {

      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to delete notification" });
    }
  });

  // Add moderation routes
  setupModerationRoutes(app);

  const httpServer = createServer(app);
  return httpServer;
}

// --- GitHub OAuth ---
app.get("/auth/github", (_req, res) => {
  const params = new URLSearchParams({
    client_id: OAUTH.clientId,
    redirect_uri: OAUTH.redirectUri,
    scope: OAUTH.scope,
    allow_signup: "true",
  });
  res.redirect(`${OAUTH.authUrl}?${params.toString()}`);
});

app.get("/auth/callback", async (req, res) => {
  const code = req.query.code as string | undefined;
  if (!code) return res.status(400).send("No code from GitHub");

  const resp = await fetch(OAUTH.tokenUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Accept": "application/json",
      "Content-Type": "application/json",
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      client_id: OAUTH.clientId,
      client_secret: OAUTH.clientSecret,
      code,
      redirect_uri: OAUTH.redirectUri,
    }),
  });

  const token = await resp.json(); // { access_token, token_type, scope, ... }
  return res.send(`<pre>${JSON.stringify(token, null, 2)}</pre>`);
});
// --- /GitHub OAuth ---

–•–æ—á–µ—à—å, —è –º–æ–≥—É –æ—Ç–º–µ—Ç–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞ —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–µ–ª–∫–∞–º–∏ ¬´–≤—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ —Å—é–¥–∞¬ª –∏ ¬´–æ—Ç—Å—Ç—É–ø –Ω–µ –Ω—É–∂–µ–Ω¬ª?

–í—ã —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∏:
–ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å –Ω–∞ –≤—Å—è–∫–∏–π –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–¥ - import type { Express } from "express";
import { createServer, type Server } from "http";
import multer from "multer";
import path from "path";
import { storage } from "./storage";
import { setupAuth, isAuthenticated } from "./replitAuth";
import { insertPostSchema, insertDocumentSchema, insertAdSchema, insertBidSchema, insertSectionSchema, insertSubsectionSchema, insertNotificationSchema } from "@shared/schema";
import { cacheMiddleware, invalidateCache } from "./middleware/cache";
import { apiLimiter, createLimiter, authLimiter } from "./middleware/rateLimiter";
import { setupModerationRoutes } from "./routes/moderation";
import express from "express";
import fetch from "node-fetch";

const OAUTH = {
  clientId: process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_ID!,
  clientSecret: process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET!,
  authUrl: process.env.OAUTH_AUTH_URL!,
  tokenUrl: process.env.OAUTH_TOKEN_URL!,
  redirectUri: process.env.OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI!,
  scope: process.env.OAUTH_SCOPE || "read:user user:email",
};


// Admin middleware
const requireAdmin = async (req: any, res: any, next: any) => {
  try {
    if (!req.user?.claims?.sub) {
      return res.status(401).json({ message: "Unauthorized" });
    }
    
    const user = await storage.getUser(req.user.claims.sub);
    if (!user || user.role !== 'admin') {
      return res.status(403).json({ message: "Admin access required" });
    }
    
    req.adminUser = user;
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Admin middleware error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ message: "Authentication error" });
  }
};

// Configure multer for file uploads
const uploadStorage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: (req, file, cb) => {
    cb(null, 'uploads/');
  },
  filename: (req, file, cb) => {
    const uniqueSuffix = Date.now() + '-' + Math.round(Math.random() * 1E9);
    cb(null, file.fieldname + '-' + uniqueSuffix + path.extname(file.originalname));
  }
});

const upload = multer({ 
  storage: uploadStorage,
  limits: {
    fileSize: 10 * 1024 * 1024, // 10MB limit
  },
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = /jpeg|jpg|png|gif|pdf|doc|docx|xls|xlsx|ppt|pptx|mp4|avi|mov|wmv|mp3|wav/;
    const extname = allowedTypes.test(path.extname(file.originalname).toLowerCase());
    const mimetype = allowedTypes.test(file.mimetype);
    
    if (mimetype && extname) {
      return cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(new Error('File type not allowed'));
    }
  }
});

export async function registerRoutes(app: Express): Promise<Server> {
  // –°—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è —Ä–∞–∑–¥–∞—á–∞ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–≤—ã—Ö —Ñ–∞–π–ª–æ–≤
  app.use('/games', express.static('games', {
    maxAge: '1d', // –ö—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ 1 –¥–µ–Ω—å
    etag: true,
    lastModified: true
  }));

  // Auth middleware
  await setupAuth(app);
  // --- GitHub OAuth ---
  app.get("/auth/github", (_req, res) => {
    const params = new URLSearchParams({
      client_id: OAUTH.clientId,
      redirect_uri: OAUTH.redirectUri,
      scope: OAUTH.scope,
      allow_signup: "true",
    });
    res.redirect(${OAUTH.authUrl}?${params.toString()});
  });

  app.get("/auth/callback", async (req, res) => {
    const code = req.query.code as string | undefined;
    if (!code) return res.status(400).send("No code from GitHub");

    const resp = await fetch(OAUTH.tokenUrl, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Accept": "application/json",
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        client_id: OAUTH.clientId,
        client_secret: OAUTH.clientSecret,
        code,
        redirect_uri: OAUTH.redirectUri,
      }),
    });

    const token = await resp.json(); // { access_token, token_type, scope, ... }
    return res.send(<pre>${JSON.stringify(token, null, 2)}</pre>);
  });
  // --- /GitHub OAuth ---


  // –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è–µ–º rate limiting –∫–æ –≤—Å–µ–º API —Ä–æ—É—Ç–∞–º
  app.use('/api', apiLimiter);
  app.use('/api/auth', authLimiter);

  // Auth routes
  app.get('/api/auth/user', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const user = await storage.getUser(userId);
      res.json(user);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching user:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch user" });
    }
  });

  // Sections routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/sections', cacheMiddleware(300), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const sections = await storage.getSections();
      res.json(sections);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching sections:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch sections" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/sections/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const section = await storage.getSection(req.params.slug);
      if (!section) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Section not found" });
      }
      res.json(section);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching section:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch section" });
    }
  });

  // Subsections routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/subsections', cacheMiddleware(300), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const sectionId = req.query.sectionId as string;
      const subsections = await storage.getSubsections(sectionId);
      res.json(subsections);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching subsections:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch subsections" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/subsections/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsection = await storage.getSubsection(req.params.slug);
      if (!subsection) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Subsection not found" });
      }
      res.json(subsection);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching subsection:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch subsection" });
    }
  });

  // Posts routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/posts', cacheMiddleware(180), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const offset = parseInt(req.query.offset as string) || 0;
      const posts = await storage.getPosts(subsectionId, limit, offset);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch posts" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/posts/featured', cacheMiddleware(600), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 5;
      const posts = await storage.getFeaturedPosts(limit);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching featured posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch featured posts" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/posts/popular', cacheMiddleware(300), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 5;
      const posts = await storage.getPopularPosts(limit);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching popular posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch popular posts" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/posts/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const post = await storage.getPost(req.params.slug);
      if (!post) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Post not found" });
      }
      
      // Increment views
      await storage.incrementPostViews(post.id);
      
      res.json(post);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching post:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch post" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/posts', isAuthenticated, createLimiter, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const postData = insertPostSchema.parse({ ...req.body, authorId: userId });
      const post = await storage.createPost(postData);
      
      // –ò–Ω–≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∫—ç—à –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ–≤
      invalidateCache('/api/posts');
      
      res.status(201).json(post);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error creating post:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to create post" });
    }
  });

  // Search routes
  app.get('/api/search', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const query = req.query.q as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      
      if (!query) {
        return res.status(400).json({ message: "Search query is required" });
      }
      
      const posts = await storage.searchPosts(query, limit);
      res.json(posts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error searching posts:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to search posts" });
    }
  });

  // Documents routes
  app.get('/api/documents', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const documents = await storage.getDocuments(subsectionId, limit);
      res.json(documents);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching documents:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch documents" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/documents/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const document = await storage.getDocument(req.params.slug);
      if (!document) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Document not found" });
      }
      res.json(document);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching document:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch document" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/documents/:id/download', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      await storage.incrementDocumentDownloads(req.params.id);
      res.json({ message: "Download count incremented" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error incrementing download count:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to increment download count" });
    }
  });

  // Photo albums routes
  app.get('/api/photo-albums', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const albums = await storage.getPhotoAlbums(subsectionId, limit);
      res.json(albums);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching photo albums:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch photo albums" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/photo-albums/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const album = await storage.getPhotoAlbum(req.params.slug);
      if (!album) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Photo album not found" });
      }
      
      const photos = await storage.getPhotosInAlbum(album.id);
      res.json({ ...album, photos });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching photo album:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch photo album" });
    }
  });

  // Videos routes
  app.get('/api/videos', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const videos = await storage.getVideos(subsectionId, limit);
      res.json(videos);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching videos:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch videos" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/videos/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const video = await storage.getVideo(req.params.slug);
      if (!video) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Video not found" });
      }
      
      // Increment views
      await storage.incrementVideoViews(video.id);
      
      res.json(video);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching video:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch video" });
    }
  });

  // Presentations routes
  app.get('/api/presentations', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const subsectionId = req.query.subsectionId as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const presentations = await storage.getPresentations(subsectionId, limit);
      res.json(presentations);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching presentations:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch presentations" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/presentations/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const presentation = await storage.getPresentation(req.params.slug);
      if (!presentation) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Presentation not found" });
      }
      
      // Increment views
      await storage.incrementPresentationViews(presentation.id);
      
      res.json(presentation);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching presentation:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch presentation" });
    }
  });

  // Marketplace routes (—Å –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º)
  app.get('/api/marketplace/categories', cacheMiddleware(600), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const categories = await storage.getAdCategories();
      console.log(Fetched ${categories.length} ad categories:, categories.map(c => c.title));
      res.json(categories);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching ad categories:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch ad categories" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/marketplace/ads', cacheMiddleware(120), async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const categoryId = req.query.categoryId as string;
      const city = req.query.city as string;
      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit as string) || 20;
      const offset = parseInt(req.query.offset as string) || 0;
      const ads = await storage.getAds(categoryId, city, limit, offset);
      res.json(ads);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching ads:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch ads" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/marketplace/ads/:slug', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const ad = await storage.getAd(req.params.slug);
      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }
      
      // Increment views
      await storage.incrementAdViews(ad.id);
      
      // Get bids for this ad
      const bids = await storage.getBids(ad.id);
      
      res.json({ ...ad, bids });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch ad" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/marketplace/ads', isAuthenticated, createLimiter, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const adData = insertAdSchema.parse({ ...req.body, userId });
      const ad = await storage.createAd(adData);
      
      // –ò–Ω–≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∏—Ä—É–µ–º –∫—ç—à –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π
      invalidateCache('/api/marketplace/ads');
      
      res.status(201).json(ad);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error creating ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to create ad" });
    }
  });

  // User dashboard routes
  app.get('/api/dashboard/ads', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const ads = await storage.getUserAds(userId);
      res.json(ads);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching user ads:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch user ads" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/dashboard/bids', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const bids = await storage.getUserBids(userId);
      res.json(bids);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching user bids:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch user bids" });
    }
  });

  // Bid routes
  app.post('/api/marketplace/ads/:adId/bids', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const adId = req.params.adId;
      const bidData = insertBidSchema.parse({ ...req.body, adId, supplierId: userId });
      const bid = await storage.createBid(bidData);
      
      // –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ–º —É–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(adId);
      if (ad) {
        await storage.createNotification({
          userId: ad.userId,
          title: '–ù–æ–≤–∞—è –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –≤–∞—à–µ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ',
          message: –ü–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ "${ad.title}",
          type: 'info',
          linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
          adId: adId,
          bidId: bid.id
        });
      }
      
      res.status(201).json(bid);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error creating bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to create bid" });
    }
  });

  app.get('/api/marketplace/ads/:adId/bids', async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const bids = await storage.getBids(req.params.adId);
      res.json(bids);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error fetching bids:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to fetch bids" });
    }
  });

  // Accept/Reject bid routes
  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:bidId/accept', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const bidId = req.params.bidId;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad || ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized" });
      }
      
      // –ü—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ–º –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É –∏ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      await storage.acceptBid(bidId, ad.id);
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: '–í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–æ!',
        message: –í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–æ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–æ,
        type: 'success',
        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
        adId: ad.id,
        bidId: bidId
      });
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤
      const allBids = await storage.getBids(ad.id);
      for (const otherBid of allBids) {
        if (otherBid.id !== bidId) {
          await storage.createNotification({
            userId: otherBid.supplierId,
            title: '–í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞–Ω–æ',
            message: –ü–æ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é "${ad.title}" –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞–Ω–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ,
            type: 'info',
            linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
            adId: ad.id,
            bidId: otherBid.id
          });
        }
      }
      
      res.json({ message: "Bid accepted successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error accepting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to accept bid" });
    }
  });

  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:bidId/reject', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const bidId = req.params.bidId;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad || ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized" });
      }
      
      // –û—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω—è–µ–º –∑–∞—è–≤–∫—É
      await storage.rejectBid(bidId);
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –ø–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤—â–∏–∫–∞
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: '–í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–æ',
        message: –í–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–æ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–æ,
        type: 'warning',
        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
        adId: ad.id,
        bidId: bidId
      });
      
      res.json({ message: "Bid rejected successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error rejecting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to reject bid" });
    }
  });

  // Close ad without selecting winner
  app.put('/api/marketplace/ads/:adId/close', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      const adId = req.params.adId;
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(adId);
      if (!ad || ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized" });
      }
      
      // –ó–∞–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ–º –æ–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ
      await storage.closeAd(adId);
      
      // –£–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª—è–µ–º –≤—Å–µ—Ö —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤
      const bids = await storage.getBids(adId);
      for (const bid of bids) {
        await storage.createNotification({
          userId: bid.supplierId,
          title: '–û–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ',
          message: –û–±—ä—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–æ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ –±–µ–∑ –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è,
          type: 'info',
          linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug},
          adId: adId,
          bidId: bid.id
        });
      }
      
      res.json({ message: "Ad closed successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error closing ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to close ad" });
    }
  });

    try {

      const uploadedFiles = [];
      
      for (const file of files) {
        const mediaData = {
          fileName: file.originalname,
          fileUrl: /uploads/${file.filename},
          fileSize: file.size,
          fileType: file.mimetype,
          uploadedBy: req.adminUser.id
        };
        const media = await storage.createMedia(mediaData);
        uploadedFiles.push(media);
      }
      
      res.status(201).json(uploadedFiles);

        { id: '2', title: '–ì–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è SEO –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–π', status: 'completed', priority: 'medium' },

  // Marketplace bid management routes
  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:id/accept', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const bidId = req.params.id;
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }

      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }

      if (ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized to manage this ad" });
      }

      await storage.acceptBid(bidId);
      
      // Create notification for accepted supplier
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: "–í–∞—à–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–∞!",
        message: –í–∞—à–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º.,
        type: "success",
        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug}
      });

      res.json({ message: "Bid accepted successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error accepting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to accept bid" });
    }
  });

  app.put('/api/marketplace/bids/:id/reject', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const bidId = req.params.id;
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      
      const bid = await storage.getBidById(bidId);
      if (!bid) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Bid not found" });
      }

      const ad = await storage.getAdById(bid.adId);
      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }

      if (ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized to manage this ad" });
      }

      await storage.rejectBid(bidId);
      
      // Create notification for rejected supplier
      await storage.createNotification({
        userId: bid.supplierId,
        title: "–ó–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–∞",
        message: –í–∞—à–∞ –∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª–∞ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–æ–Ω–µ–Ω–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º.,
        type: "warning",
        linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug}
      });

      res.json({ message: "Bid rejected successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error rejecting bid:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to reject bid" });
    }
  });

  app.put('/api/marketplace/ads/:id/close', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const adId = req.params.id;
      const userId = req.user.claims.sub;
      
      const ad = await storage.getAdById(adId);
      if (!ad) {
        return res.status(404).json({ message: "Ad not found" });
      }

      if (ad.userId !== userId) {
        return res.status(403).json({ message: "Not authorized to manage this ad" });
      }

      await storage.closeAd(adId);
      
      // Create notifications for all bidders
      const bids = await storage.getBidsForAd(adId);
      for (const bid of bids) {
        if (bid.status === 'pending') {
          await storage.createNotification({
            userId: bid.supplierId,
            title: "–ó–∞–∫–∞–∑ –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç",
            message: –ó–∞–∫–∞–∑ "${ad.title}" –±—ã–ª –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç –∑–∞–∫–∞–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º –±–µ–∑ –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è.,
            type: "info",
            linkUrl: /marketplace/ads/${ad.slug}
          });
        }
      }

      res.json({ message: "Ad closed successfully" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error closing ad:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to close ad" });
    }
  });



  app.post('/api/notifications', isAuthenticated, requireAdmin, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      const notificationData = insertNotificationSchema.parse(req.body);
      const notification = await storage.createNotification(notificationData);
      res.status(201).json(notification);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error creating notification:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to create notification" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/notifications/:id/read', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      await storage.markNotificationAsRead(req.params.id, req.user.claims.sub);
      res.json({ message: "Notification marked as read" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error marking notification as read:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to mark as read" });
    }
  });

  app.post('/api/notifications/mark-all-read', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      await storage.markAllNotificationsAsRead(req.user.claims.sub);
      res.json({ message: "All notifications marked as read" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error marking all notifications as read:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to mark all as read" });
    }
  });

  app.delete('/api/notifications/:id', isAuthenticated, async (req: any, res) => {
    try {
      await storage.deleteNotification(req.params.id, req.user.claims.sub);
      res.json({ message: "Notification deleted" });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error deleting notification:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ message: "Failed to delete notification" });
    }
  });

  // Add moderation routes
  setupModerationRoutes(app);

  const httpServer = createServer(app);
  return httpServer;
}

OAUTH_AUTH_URL / OAUTH_TOKEN_URL ‚Äî –¥–ª—è —Ç–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±—ç–∫–µ–Ω–¥–∞ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å GitHub-–æ–≤—Å–∫–∏–µ:

https://github.com/login/oauth/authorize

https://github.com/login/oauth/access_token

https://‚Ä¶replit.dev/auth/callback (–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞ —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω–µ ‚Äî —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å —ç—Ç–æ –≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ –¥–ª—è —Ç–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ /auth/github)

GPT Action authentication
=========================

Learn authentication options for GPT Actions.

Actions offer different authentication schemas to accommodate various use cases. To specify the authentication schema for your action, use the GPT editor and select "None", "API Key", or "OAuth".

By default, the authentication method for all actions is set to "None", but you can change this and allow different actions to have different authentication methods.

No authentication
-----------------

We support flows without authentication for applications where users can send requests directly to your API without needing an API key or signing in with OAuth.

Consider using no authentication for initial user interactions as you might experience a user drop off if they are forced to sign into an application. You can create a "signed out" experience and then move users to a "signed in" experience by enabling a separate action.

API key authentication
----------------------

Just like how a user might already be using your API, we allow API key authentication through the GPT editor UI. We encrypt the secret key when we store it in our database to keep your API key secure.

This approach is useful if you have an API that takes slightly more consequential actions than the no authentication flow but does not require an individual user to sign in. Adding API key authentication can protect your API and give you more fine-grained access controls along with visibility into where requests are coming from.

OAuth
-----

Actions allow OAuth sign in for each user. This is the best way to provide personalized experiences and make the most powerful actions available to users. A simple example of the OAuth flow with actions will look like the following:

*   To start, select "Authentication" in the GPT editor UI, and select "OAuth".
*   You will be prompted to enter the OAuth client ID, client secret, authorization URL, token URL, and scope.
    *   The client ID and secret can be simple text strings but should [follow OAuth best practices](https://www.oauth.com/oauth2-servers/client-registration/client-id-secret/).
    *   We store an encrypted version of the client secret, while the client ID is available to end users.
*   OAuth requests will include the following information: request={'grant_type': 'authorization_code', 'client_id': 'YOUR_CLIENT_ID', 'client_secret': 'YOUR_CLIENT_SECRET', 'code': 'abc123', 'redirect_uri': 'https://chat.openai.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback'} Note: https://chatgpt.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback is also valid.
*   In order for someone to use an action with OAuth, they will need to send a message that invokes the action and then the user will be presented with a "Sign in to \[domain\]" button in the ChatGPT UI.
*   The authorization_url endpoint should return a response that looks like: { "access_token": "example_token", "token_type": "bearer", "refresh_token": "example_token", "expires_in": 59 }
*   During the user sign in process, ChatGPT makes a request to your authorization_url using the specified authorization_content_type, we expect to get back an access token and optionally a [refresh token](https://auth0.com/learn/refresh-tokens) which we use to periodically fetch a new access token.
*   Each time a user makes a request to the action, the user‚Äôs token will be passed in the Authorization header: ("Authorization": "\[Bearer/Basic\] \[user‚Äôs token\]").
*   We require that OAuth applications make use of the [state parameter](https://auth0.com/docs/secure/attack-protection/state-parameters#set-and-compare-state-parameter-values) for security reasons.

Failure to login issues on Custom GPTs (Redirect URLs)?

*   Be sure to enable this redirect URL in your OAuth application:
*   #1 Redirect URL: https://chat.openai.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback (Different domain possible for some clients)
*   #2 Redirect URL: https://chatgpt.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback (Get your GPT ID in the URL bar of the ChatGPT UI once you save) if you have several GPTs you'd need to enable for each or a wildcard depending on risk tolerance.
*   Debug Note: Your Auth Provider will typically log failures (e.g. 'redirect\_uri is not registered for client'), which helps debug login issues as well.
ChatGPT —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª:

–ü–æ–Ω—è–ª üëç
–ß—Ç–æ–±—ã OAuth –≤ Custom GPT —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–ª –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ, —Ç–µ–±–µ –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Å–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –æ–±–∞ Redirect URL –≤ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∞—Ö OAuth-–ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è.

–í–æ—Ç —Ç–æ—á–Ω—ã–µ —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫–∏ (–∏—Ö –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –≤–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫ –µ—Å—Ç—å, —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–æ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–π GPT-ID –≤–º–µ—Å—Ç–æ {g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}):

https://chat.openai.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback

ChatGPT —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª:

–°—É–ø–µ—Ä üëç

–®–∞–≥ 6

–ù–∞–∂–º–∏ –≤–Ω–∏–∑—É –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫—É ¬´–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω¬ª (Generate token).

–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ—è–≤–∏—Ç—Å—è —Å–∞–º —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω (–¥–ª–∏–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∞). –ï–≥–æ –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É —Å–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä—É–π –∏ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏ –≤ –±–ª–æ–∫–Ω–æ—Ç, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º GitHub –µ–≥–æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç.

–°–¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—à—å ‚Äî —Å–∫–∏–Ω—å —Å–∫—Ä–∏–Ω.

–í—ã —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∏:
–Ω–µ—Ç—É —Å–ª–æ–≤–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω, –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å! –∞ –ø—Ä–∏ –Ω–∞–∂–∞—Ç–∏–∏ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∏ –Ω–∞ –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç - GPT Action authentication
=========================

Learn authentication options for GPT Actions.

Actions offer different authentication schemas to accommodate various use cases. To specify the authentication schema for your action, use the GPT editor and select "None", "API Key", or "OAuth".

By default, the authentication method for all actions is set to "None", but you can change this and allow different actions to have different authentication methods.

No authentication
-----------------

We support flows without authentication for applications where users can send requests directly to your API without needing an API key or signing in with OAuth.

Consider using no authentication for initial user interactions as you might experience a user drop off if they are forced to sign into an application. You can create a "signed out" experience and then move users to a "signed in" experience by enabling a separate action.

API key authentication
----------------------

Just like how a user might already be using your API, we allow API key authentication through the GPT editor UI. We encrypt the secret key when we store it in our database to keep your API key secure.

This approach is useful if you have an API that takes slightly more consequential actions than the no authentication flow but does not require an individual user to sign in. Adding API key authentication can protect your API and give you more fine-grained access controls along with visibility into where requests are coming from.

OAuth
-----

Actions allow OAuth sign in for each user. This is the best way to provide personalized experiences and make the most powerful actions available to users. A simple example of the OAuth flow with actions will look like the following:

*   To start, select "Authentication" in the GPT editor UI, and select "OAuth".
*   You will be prompted to enter the OAuth client ID, client secret, authorization URL, token URL, and scope.
    *   The client ID and secret can be simple text strings but should [follow OAuth best practices](https://www.oauth.com/oauth2-servers/client-registration/client-id-secret/).
    *   We store an encrypted version of the client secret, while the client ID is available to end users.
*   OAuth requests will include the following information: request={'grant_type': 'authorization_code', 'client_id': 'YOUR_CLIENT_ID', 'client_secret': 'YOUR_CLIENT_SECRET', 'code': 'abc123', 'redirect_uri': 'https://chat.openai.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback'} Note: https://chatgpt.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback is also valid.
*   In order for someone to use an action with OAuth, they will need to send a message that invokes the action and then the user will be presented with a "Sign in to \[domain\]" button in the ChatGPT UI.
*   The authorization_url endpoint should return a response that looks like: { "access_token": "example_token", "token_type": "bearer", "refresh_token": "example_token", "expires_in": 59 }
*   During the user sign in process, ChatGPT makes a request to your authorization_url using the specified authorization_content_type, we expect to get back an access token and optionally a [refresh token](https://auth0.com/learn/refresh-tokens) which we use to periodically fetch a new access token.
*   Each time a user makes a request to the action, the user‚Äôs token will be passed in the Authorization header: ("Authorization": "\[Bearer/Basic\] \[user‚Äôs token\]").
*   We require that OAuth applications make use of the [state parameter](https://auth0.com/docs/secure/attack-protection/state-parameters#set-and-compare-state-parameter-values) for security reasons.

Failure to login issues on Custom GPTs (Redirect URLs)?

*   Be sure to enable this redirect URL in your OAuth application:
*   #1 Redirect URL: https://chat.openai.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback (Different domain possible for some clients)
*   #2 Redirect URL: https://chatgpt.com/aip/{g-YOUR-GPT-ID-HERE}/oauth/callback (Get your GPT ID in the URL bar of the ChatGPT UI once you save) if you have several GPTs you'd need to enable for each or a wildcard depending on risk tolerance.
*   Debug Note: Your Auth Provider will typically log failures (e.g. 'redirect\_uri is not registered for client'), which helps debug login issues as well.

paths:

      summary: Create a repository in the authenticated user's account
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [name, private]
              properties:
                name:
                  type: string
                  description: Repository name
                private:
                  type: boolean
                  description: Whether the repository is private
      responses:

          description: Repository created
        "422":
          description: Validation failed
  /repos/{owner}/{repo}/contents/{path}:

      summary: Create or update a file's contents
      description: Uses GitHub Contents API to create/update a file. The content must be Base64-encoded.

        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - in: path
          name: owner
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
        - in: path
          name: repo
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
        - in: path
          name: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            description: File path within the repo (e.g., README.md or src/index.js)
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required: [message, content]
              properties:

                  type: string
                  description: Commit message
                content:
                  type: string
                  description: Base64-encoded file content

                  type: string
                  description: Target branch (default main if omitted)

–í –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–µ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω—ã –≤—Å–ø–ª—ã–≤–∞—é—â–∏–µ –æ–∫–Ω–∞ –¥–ª—è chatgpt.com –∏ github.com.

–ü–æ—Å–ª–µ –∑–∞–º–µ–Ω—ã callback Client secret –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –±—ã—Ç—å —Å–≤–µ–∂–∏–º (—Å—Ç–∞—Ä—ã–π –Ω–µ–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª–µ–Ω).

–í GPT Editor –ø–æ–ª—è Client ID / Secret –±–µ–∑ –ø—Ä–æ–±–µ–ª–æ–≤ –≤ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–µ/–∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ.

–ï—Å–ª–∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—à—å –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç GitHub ‚Äî –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—å, —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∏–∫–∞ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–∞–µ—Ç OAuth-–ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—é –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –∫ —Ä–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è–º.

–ë—ã—Å—Ç—Ä—ã–π —Ç–µ—Å—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –≤—Å—ë –æ–∫

–°–∫–∞–∂–∏ —Å–≤–æ–µ–º—É GPT:

¬´–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–π —Ä–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–π gpt-replit-test-ok (public) –∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å —Ñ–∞–π–ª hello.txt —Å–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–æ–π ‚ÄúHello from GPT ‚úÖ‚Äù (–∫–æ–º–º–∏—Ç: feat: add hello.txt).¬ª

–û–∂–∏–¥–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç: GPT –ø–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ–¥–∏–Ω —Ä–∞–∑, –∑–∞—Ç–µ–º –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–∏—Ç ‚Äú–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–æ‚Äù –∏ —É–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫—É –Ω–∞ —Ä–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–π —Å —Ñ–∞–π–ª–æ–º.

–ü—Ä–æ –±–µ–∑–æ–ø–∞—Å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å

–¢—ã –≤—ã—à–µ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–ª –ª–æ–≥–∏–Ω—ã/–ø–∞—Ä–æ–ª–∏ ‚Äî –æ—á–µ–Ω—å —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ç—É—é –∏—Ö —Å–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å (–∏ –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å 2FA), —Ç.–∫. —ç—Ç–æ —á—É–≤—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ. –Ø –∏—Ö –Ω–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é –∏ –Ω–µ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è—é, –Ω–æ —Ñ–∞–∫—Ç –ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ ‚Äî —Ä–∏—Å–∫.

–ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ö–æ—á–µ—à—å, —è –º–æ–≥—É –æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞ –ª–∏–Ω–∏–∏ –∏ ‚Äú–ø—Ä–æ–π—Ç–∏ —Å —Ç–æ–±–æ–π‚Äù —ç—Ç–∏ —à–∞–≥–∏: —Ç—ã –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—à—å —à–∞–≥ ‚Üí –ø–∏—à–µ—à—å, —á—Ç–æ –≤–∏–¥–∏—à—å/–∫—É–¥–∞ –Ω–∞–∂–∞–ª ‚Üí —è –¥–∞—é —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–π –∫–æ—Ä–æ—Ç–∫–∏–π —à–∞–≥. –≠—Ç–æ –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç 3‚Äì5 –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç.
